country_event = { # Mission: Crush Prussia
	id = gerspd.15
	title = gerspd.15.t
	desc = gerspd.15.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_prussia

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerspd.15 option gerspd.15.a"
		name = gerspd.15.a
		add_ideas = GER_prussian_budget_crisis
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
					add_idea = GER_paralysis_base
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = -0.05 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
				max = 0
				min = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.69 } # AI cheat
					}
					AND = {
						is_ai = no
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.49 }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = gerspd.53
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = EFFECT_UNLOCK_DECISION_CATEGORY
			NAME = GER_prussian_budget_crisis
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = { GER_prussia_victories = 0 } # Need at least 3 (of 4?) to claim victory.
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_prussian_budget_crisis_defeat
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_mp_schleicher }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_schleicher_negotiate }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_agriculture_concessions }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_national_liberals }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_house_boycott }
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_prussia_adenauer_communication }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # New Prussia Election
	id = gerspd.22
	title = gerspd.22.t
	desc = gerspd.22.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_prussia

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerspd.22 option gerspd.22.a"
		name = gerspd.22.a # Unpopular policy, but it brings a few seats for SPD.
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Right_seats = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_LVP_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 5 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats = 2 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_NLP_seats = 2 }

		hidden_effect = {
			# Results processing.
			set_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Left_seats }
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_LVP_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Polish_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_agrarians_in_coalition
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Agrarian_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_Prussian_NLP_support
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_NLP_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition > 221 }
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = gerspd.23 days = 3 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = gerspd.24 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerspd.22 option gerspd.22.b"
		name = gerspd.22.b # Makes very little change.
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_Right_seats = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_Left_seats = 3 }
		subtract_from_variable = { GER_Prussia_DkP_seats = 3 }
		add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_LVP_seats = 3 }

		hidden_effect = {
			# Results processing.
			set_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Left_seats }
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_LVP_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes }
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Zentrum_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Polish_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_agrarians_in_coalition
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_Agrarian_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_Prussian_NLP_support
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition = GER_Prussia_NLP_seats }
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { GER_Prussia_coalition > 221 }
						is_ai = yes
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = gerspd.23 days = 3 }
			}
			else = {
				country_event = { id = gerspd.24 days = 3 }
			}
		}
	}
}

			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.69 } # AI cheat
					}
					AND = {
						is_ai = no
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.49 }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = gerspd.53
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_schleicher_endorses_brunswick_front_tt
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_iron_front_topple_schleicher }
	}
}

country_event = { # The Brunswick Front - Papen endorsement
	id = gerspd.45
	title = gerspd.45.t
	desc = gerspd.45.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_papen

	trigger = {
		is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerspd.45 option gerspd.45.a"
		name = gerspd.45.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
					add_idea = GER_paralysis_base
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = -0.05 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
				max = 0
				min = -1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
				OR = {
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.69 } # AI cheat
					}
					AND = {
						is_ai = no
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.49 }
					}
				}
			}
			country_event = gerspd.53
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_Z_loyalty
			value = 10
			tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
				is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Z_rift
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_papen_active_brunswick
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_SPD_iron_front_topple_papen }
	}
}

country_event = { # Fall of the Government
	id = gerspd.52
	immediate = {
		log = "KR_Event_Logging;GER Political Path - Schwander Cabinet"
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = GER_schwander_party_long
				name = GER_schwander_party
			}
		}
	}
	title = gerspd.52.t
	desc = gerspd.52.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_schwander

	trigger = {
		NOT = {
			AND = {
				is_ai = yes
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_DU_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_DU_SOCCON }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerspd.52 option gerspd.52.a"
		name = gerspd.52.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_rudolf_schwander = { set_nationality = ROOT }
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_rudolf_schwander_sic
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_liberal
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_schwander_government_happened
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		remove_mission = GER_coalition_relations
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_paralysis_base
					add_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_10
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = 0.1 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
				max = 0
				min = -1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor > -0.01 }
				}
				country_event = gerspd.69
			}
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		hidden_effect = { country_event = gerspd.64 }
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerspd.54 option gerspd.54.a"
		name = gerspd.54.a
		add_stability = -0.1
		add_political_power = 150
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
			}
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_paralysis_base
					add_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
				}
			}
			add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = 0.05 }
			clamp_variable = {
				var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
				max = 0
				min = -1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor > -0.01 }
				}
				country_event = gerspd.69
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_free_political_advisor_slot = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GER_hofgeismar_circle = { set_nationality = ROOT }
				activate_advisor = GER_hofgeismar_circle_advisor
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = if_not_yet_hired_will_hire
			show_ideas_tooltip = GER_hofgeismar_circle_advisor
		}
		else = {
			add_ideas = GER_SPD_rebellion
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_Z_loyalty
			value = 20
			tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }

			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
				is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
			}

		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_LVP_loyalty
			value = 20
			tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty < 1 }
				is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_LVP_rift
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_Polish_loyalty
			value = 20
			tooltip = GER_Polish_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_Polish_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty < 1 }
				has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Polish_rift

						has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
					}
				}

			}

					count_triggers = {
						amount = 3
						has_completed_focus = GER_service_law_democracy
						check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty > 59 }
						check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty > 59 }
						NOT = {
							has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = gerspd.67
			}
			else = {
				country_event = gerspd.68
			}
		}
	}
	option = {

		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_prussia_equal_suffrage_chances_2_tt

							amount = 2

							check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty > 59 }
							NOT = {
								has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
							}
						}
						count_triggers = {
							amount = 3
							has_completed_focus = GER_service_law_democracy
							check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty > 59 }
							check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty > 59 }
							NOT = {
								has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
							}
						}
						AND = {
							has_completed_focus = GER_service_law_democracy
							check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty > 59 }
							check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty > 59 }
							NOT = {
								has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
							}
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = gerspd.66
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = GER_service_law_democracy
						check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty > 59 }
						check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty > 59 }
						NOT = {
							has_active_mission = GER_brunswick_front_activity
						}
					}
				}
				country_event = gerspd.67
			}
			else = {
				country_event = gerspd.68
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Tensions in the Iron Front
	id = gerspd.79
	title = gerspd.79.t
	desc = gerspd.79.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_ruhruprising

	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		has_active_mission = GER_iron_front_activity
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				seed = global.date
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = gerspd.79 days = 40 random_days = 10 }
				}
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = gerspd.80 days = 40 random_days = 10 }
				}
				33 = {
					country_event = { id = gerspd.81 days = 40 random_days = 10 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerspd.79 option gerspd.79.a"
		name = gerspd.79.a
		ai_chance = { base = 10 }
		add_political_power = -25
		add_to_variable = { GER_iron_front_organisation = -10 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_10_iron_front_organisation_loss
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerspd.79 option gerspd.79.b"
		name = gerspd.79.b
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty
			value = 10
			tooltip = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Left_SPD_loyalty < 1 }
				has_country_flag = GER_left_spd_in_coalition
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Left_rift
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_Z_loyalty
			value = 10
			tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
				is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Z_rift
		}
	}
}

			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Left_rift

country_event = { # Military stuff
	id = germil.1
	title = germil.1.t
	desc = germil.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_army

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event germil.1 option germil.1.a"
		name = germil.1.a
		set_country_flag = GER_military_mechanics_unlocked
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_military_mechanics_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_du_path = yes
				}
				set_variable = { GER_military_faction_strength = 20 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_swr_path = yes
				}
				set_variable = { GER_military_faction_strength = 50 }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
				}
				set_variable = { GER_military_faction_strength = 30 }
			}
			unlock_national_focus = GER_army_reform_stuff
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #hidden event to trigger Wilhelm's death even if GER is dead
	id = gerflavour.8

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = 64.owner #this needs to be a MTTH due to the variance in GER scenarios
		date > 1941.6.4
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.8 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_leader = { character = GER_wilhelm_ii } }
			country_event = gerflavour.9
			news_event = { id = gerflavour.118 days = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = MAF
				MAF = { has_country_leader = { character = GER_wilhelm_ii } }
			}
			MAF = {
				country_event = gerflavour.9
				news_event = { id = gerflavour.118 days = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			GER_wilhelm_ii_dies = yes
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Death of Wilhelm II
	id = gerflavour.9
	title = gerflavour.9.t
	desc = {
		text = gerflavour.9.d_GER
		trigger = {
			tag = GER
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = gerflavour.9.d_GEX
		trigger = {
			tag = MAF
		}
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_willy_dead

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.9 option gerflavour.9.a"
		name = gerflavour.9.a
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_wilhelm_ii_dies = yes

country_event = { # The [Year] German Elections
	id = gerflavour.25
	title = gerflavour.25.t
	desc = gerflavour.25.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_ser_election

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = GER_von_schleicher_cabinet
	}
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				long_name = GER_social_liberal_party_long
				name = GER_social_liberal_party
			}
		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.25 option gerflavour.25.a"
		name = gerflavour.25.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				GER_is_du_path = yes
				has_country_flag = GER_swr_path_goes_to_democracy
				has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_path_goes_to_democracy
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_DU_SOCDEM }
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SOCLIB }
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_postwar_elections_held
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_conservative
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_women_suffrage
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_women_suffrage_event
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_women_suffrage_event
			country_event = gerflavour.108
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_completed_focus = GER_protect_states_rights }
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_carl_ulitzka_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_compromise_board
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_konrad_adenauer_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_centre_chairman
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_adam_stegerwald_sic
		}
		else = {
			activate_advisor = GER_fritz_schaffer_sic
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.25 option gerflavour.25.b"
		name = gerflavour.25.b
		trigger = {
			GER_is_du_path = yes
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_DU_SOCCON }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_women_suffrage
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_women_suffrage_event
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = GER_women_suffrage_event
			country_event = gerflavour.108
		}
		set_country_flag = GER_postwar_elections_held
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = social_democrat
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_theodor_haubach_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.25 option gerflavour.25.c1"
		name = gerflavour.25.c1
		trigger = {
			GER_is_swr_path = yes
			GER_paul_lejeune_jung = { is_second_in_command = no }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_failed_swr_government }
			has_country_flag = GER_treviranus_co_chair
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SWR_PATAUT }
					has_country_flag = GER_dvlp_ai
				}
			}
		}
		GER_postwar_swr_elected_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { GER_gottfried_treviranus = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
		activate_advisor = GER_gottfried_treviranus_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.25 option gerflavour.25.c2"
		name = gerflavour.25.c2
		trigger = {
			GER_is_swr_path = yes
			GER_paul_lejeune_jung = { is_second_in_command = no }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_failed_swr_government }
			has_country_flag = GER_schlange_co_chair
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SWR_PATAUT }
					has_country_flag = GER_dvlp_ai
				}
			}
		}
		GER_postwar_swr_elected_effect = yes
		GER_hans_schlange_schoningen = {
			hidden_effect = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			remove_political_advisor_role = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_hans_schlange_schoningen_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.25 option gerflavour.25.c3"
		name = gerflavour.25.c3
		trigger = {
			GER_is_swr_path = yes
			GER_paul_lejeune_jung = { is_second_in_command = no }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_failed_swr_government }
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 100
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SWR_AUTDEM }
					has_country_flag = GER_dkp_ai
				}
			}
		}
		GER_postwar_swr_elected_effect = yes
		activate_advisor = GER_ulrich_von_hassell_sic
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.25 option gerflavour.25.e"
		name = gerflavour.25.e
		trigger = {
			GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { is_second_in_command = yes }
			NOT = { has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_path_goes_to_democracy }
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			election_frequency = 60
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.25 option gerflavour.25.f"
		trigger = {
			NOT = { has_cosmetic_tag = GER_rep }
			has_country_leader = { character = GER_wilhelm_iv }

				}
			}
		}
		name = gerflavour.25.f
		set_country_flag = GER_postwar_elections_held
		set_politics = {

country_event = { # Elections delayed
	id = gerflavour.28
	title = gerflavour.28.t
	desc = gerflavour.28.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_remove_france

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.28 option gerflavour.28.a"
		name = gerflavour.28.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes }
				set_country_flag = GER_has_soclib_coalition
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_market_liberal = yes }
				set_country_flag = GER_has_marklib_coalition
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes }
				set_country_flag = GER_has_soccon_coalition
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_authoritarian_democrat = yes }
				set_country_flag = GER_has_authdem_coalition
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_paternal_autocrat = yes }
				set_country_flag = GER_has_pataut_coalition
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_national_populist = yes }
				set_country_flag = GER_has_natpop_coalition
			}
			meta_effect = {
				text = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = var:current_party_ideology_group
						last_election = "[CURRENT_DATE]"
						election_frequency = 12
						elections_allowed = yes
					}
				}
				CURRENT_DATE = "[?global.date.GetDateStringNoHour]"
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_soclib_coalition
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_liberal }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_marklib_coalition
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:market_liberal }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_soccon_coalition
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_authdem_coalition
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_pataut_coalition
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_has_natpop_coalition
				}
				set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
				add_to_coalition = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

news_event = {
	id = gerflavour.35
	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.35" }
	title = gerflavour.35.t

	desc = gerflavour.35.d

	picture = GFX_news_event_GER_schleicher_cabinet

	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gerflavour.35.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				is_ally_with = INT
				is_ally_with = RUS
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gerflavour.35.b
		trigger = { is_ally_with = GER }
	}
	option = {
		name = gerflavour.35.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { is_ally_with = INT }
			has_socialist_government = no
			NOT = { is_ally_with = GER }
			NOT = { is_ally_with = RUS }
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # National People's Union - Moderate
	id = gerflavour.41
	title = gerflavour.41.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_schlange_co_chair
		}
		text = gerflavour.41.d1
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = GER_treviranus_co_chair
		}
		text = gerflavour.41.d2
	}
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_westarp

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.41 option gerflavour.41.a"
		name = gerflavour.41.a
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = authoritarian_democrat
			elections_allowed = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_kuno_von_westarp = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_dnvu_long
				name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_dnvu
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_dnvu_long2
				name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_dnvu
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
						has_country_flag = GER_federalist_union_established
					}
				}
				country_event = gerflavour.102
			}
		}
		GER_ulrich_von_hassell = {
			remove_political_advisor_role = yes
		}
		effect_tooltip = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
				long_name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_dnvu_long_fake
				name = GER_authoritarian_democrat_party_dnvu
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_dnvu_long2_fake
				name = GER_paternal_autocrat_party_dnvu
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:paternal_autocrat }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = national_populist
			long_name = GER_national_populist_party_dnvu_long
			name = GER_national_populist_party_dnvu
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_treviranus_co_chair
			}
			hidden_effect = { GER_gottfried_treviranus = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
			activate_advisor = GER_gottfried_treviranus_sic
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_schlange_co_chair
			}
			GER_hans_schlange_schoningen = {
				hidden_effect = { set_nationality = ROOT }
				remove_political_advisor_role = yes
			}
			activate_advisor = GER_hans_schlange_schoningen_sic
		}
		else = { # just in case
			activate_advisor = GER_kuno_von_westarp_sic
		}
	}
}

	desc = gerflavour.53.d

		OR = {

			AND = {
				GER_is_swr_path = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
				}
			}
			AND = {
				GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
				}
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = GER_bauer_putsch
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.53 option gerflavour.53.a"
		name = gerflavour.53.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			popularity = 0.02
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = social_conservative
			long_name = GER_social_conservative_party_long_cvp
			name = GER_social_conservative_party_cvp
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_conservative }
		remove_from_coalition = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_compromise_board
				}
				country_event = gerflavour.54
			}
		}
	}

country_event = { # Schleicher's Retirement
	id = gerflavour.55
	title = gerflavour.55.t
	desc = gerflavour.55.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_schleicher9

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = gerflavour.56 days = 120 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.55 option gerflavour.55.a"
		name = gerflavour.55.a
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { retire = yes }
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_ferdinand_von_bredow = { set_nationality = ROOT }
			unlock_national_focus = GER_nationalise_prussian_secret_police
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_ferdinand_von_bredow_sic

		# Turn you paternal_autocrat if you filled out the New State decisions.
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_idea = GER_new_state_6
					AND = {
						is_ai = yes
						has_game_rule = { rule = GER_path option = GER_PATH_SCHLEICHER_PATAUT }
					}
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = authoritarian_democrat
					popularity = -0.3
				}
				add_popularity = {
					ideology = paternal_autocrat
					popularity = 0.3
				}
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
				elections_allowed = no
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:authoritarian_democrat }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
			add_to_coalition = yes
			hidden_effect = {
				GER_increase_new_state_to_end = yes
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_red_general_absorb_aspd_flag
			}
			set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:social_democrat }

			GER_tilo_wilmowsky = {
				set_nationality = ROOT

			}
		}

	title = gerflavour.79.t
	desc = gerflavour.79.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_reemtsma

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.79 option gerflavour.79.a"
		name = gerflavour.79.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = -0.04
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER_is_du_path = yes
			}
			add_stability = 0.02
			if = {
				limit = {
					is_in_array = { GER.democratic_union_members_array = 9.id } # has Zentrum (Centre)
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					# Z gains 1 MP
					add_to_variable = { GER_Z_seats_in_coalition = 1 }
					add_to_variable = { GER_du_coalition_number = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER_is_swr_path = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dkp_tt
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = -10 }
			GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_zentrum_deputies = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_r = 1 }
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
						has_country_flag = GER_federalist_union_established
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number = 1 }
				# If coalition number is now under 50%+1 of the Reichstag, start the failstate
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_number < 223 }
					}
					country_event = gerswr.32
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_goering_resigns_tt
		}
	}
}

	immediate = { log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.84" }
	title = {
		trigger = {
			GER = { has_war_with = JAP }
			JAP = { is_subject = no }
		}
		text = gerflavour.84.t1
	}
	title = {
		trigger = { GER = { has_war_with = CHI } }
		text = gerflavour.84.t2
	}
	desc = { #Japan Signs Peace with Germany
		text = gerflavour.84.d1
		trigger = {
			GER = { has_war_with = JAP }
			JAP = { is_subject = no }
		}
	}
	desc = { #CHI Signs Peace with Germany
		text = gerflavour.84.d2
		trigger = { GER = { has_war_with = CHI } }
	}
	picture = GFX_news_event_JAP_germany_peace
	major = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	option = { #Germany
		name = gerflavour.84.a
		trigger = { tag = GER }
	}
	option = { #Japan
		name = gerflavour.84.b
		trigger = { tag = JAP }
	}
	option = { #Entente
		name = gerflavour.84.c
		trigger = { is_in_faction_with = ENT }
	}
	option = { #RUS
		name = gerflavour.84.e
		trigger = {
			tag = RUS
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
	}
	option = { #Socialist
		name = gerflavour.84.f
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
			NOT = { tag = CHI }
		}
	}
	option = { #Generic
		name = gerflavour.84.g
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				tag = GER
				tag = JAP
				is_in_faction_with = ENT
				tag = RUS
				has_socialist_government = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #the true based option
		name = gerflavour.84.h
		trigger = {
			tag = CHI
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Women's suffrage?
	id = gerflavour.93
	title = gerflavour.93.t
	desc = gerflavour.93.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_suffrags

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.93 option gerflavour.93.a"
		name = gerflavour.93.a
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		trigger = {
			GER_is_du_path = yes
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_right_chairman
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Z_loyalty
				value = 20
				tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Z_loyalty
				value = 10
				tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
				is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Z_rift
		}
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_Polish_loyalty
			value = 10
			tooltip = GER_Polish_loyalty_loss
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_Polish_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_Polish_loyalty < 1 }
				has_country_flag = GER_poles_in_coalition
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_Polish_rift
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
			days = 30
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.93 option gerflavour.93.b"
		name = gerflavour.93.b
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		trigger = {
			GER_is_du_path = yes
		}
		add_political_power = 10
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = SPD_left_LVP_boosted
			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_LVP_loyalty
				value = 15
				tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		}
		else = {
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_LVP_loyalty
				value = 10
				tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
			}
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty < 1 }
				is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes
			}
			activate_mission = GER_SPD_LVP_rift
		}
		add_days_mission_timeout = {
			mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
			days = -30
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.93 option gerflavour.93.c"
		name = gerflavour.93.c
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		trigger = {
			GER_is_schleicher_path = yes
		}
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_red_general_local_women_suffrage }
		activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_red_general_reichsfrauenbund }
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.93 option gerflavour.93.e"
		name = gerflavour.93.e
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				has_country_flag = GER_schleicher_ai
			}
		}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				GER_is_du_path = yes
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.02
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Hilfspolizei
	id = gerflavour.95
	title = gerflavour.95.t
	desc = gerflavour.95.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_march

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.95 option gerflavour.95.a"
		name = gerflavour.95.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.03
		}
		add_war_support = 0.03
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
				NOT = { check_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier < -0.02 } }
			}
			remove_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Lacking_Preparedness }
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier
			clear_variable = GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2
		}
		else = {
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier = 0.02 }
			add_to_variable = { GER_lacking_preparedness_modifier_2 = 0.01 }
			effect_tooltip = {
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = GER_unprepared_none
					add_idea = GER_unprepared_reduction
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.95 option gerflavour.95.b"
		name = gerflavour.95.b
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
	}
}

country_event = { # UKR accepts
	id = gerflavour.104
	title = gerflavour.104.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_left_spd_demands_5
		}
		text = gerflavour.104.d1 # Seydewitz
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_flag = GER_left_spd_has_split
				has_government = social_liberal
			}
		}
		text = gerflavour.104.d2 # Sollmann
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 4
		}
		text = gerflavour.104.d3 # Schärf (Austrian)
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			has_completed_focus = GER_tarnow_baade_plan
		}
		text = gerflavour.104.d4 # Baade
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = GER_left_spd_demands_5
					has_country_flag = GER_left_spd_has_split
					has_government = social_liberal
					owns_state = 4
					has_completed_focus = GER_tarnow_baade_plan
				}
			}
		}
		text = gerflavour.104.d5 # Naphtali
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { # Nice
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.104 option gerflavour.104.a"
		name = gerflavour.104.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_left_spd_demands_5
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = radical_socialist
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			hidden_effect = { GER_max_seydewitz = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = GER_max_seydewitz_advisor
			custom_effect_tooltip = is_hired
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_free_political_advisor_slot = yes
					}
					activate_advisor = GER_max_seydewitz_advisor
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_seydewitz_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = GER_left_spd_has_split
					has_government = social_liberal
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_liberal
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			hidden_effect = { GER_wilhelm_sollmann = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = GER_wilhelm_sollmann_advisor
			custom_effect_tooltip = is_hired
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_free_political_advisor_slot = yes
					}
					activate_advisor = GER_wilhelm_sollmann_advisor
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_sollmann_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 4
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = social_democrat
				popularity = 0.03
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_austria = yes
					is_owned_by = GER
				}
				add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_SPDA_Stronghold }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_scharf_tt
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_tarnow_baade_plan
			}
			hidden_effect = { GER_fritz_baade = { set_nationality = ROOT } } # already recruited previously, but shouldn't break anything, and the player may have forgotten.
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = GER_fritz_baade_advisor
			custom_effect_tooltip = is_hired
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_free_political_advisor_slot = yes
					}
					activate_advisor = GER_fritz_baade_advisor
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_baade_tt
		}
		else = {
			hidden_effect = { GER_fritz_naphtali = { set_nationality = ROOT } }
			custom_effect_tooltip = available_political_advisor
			show_ideas_tooltip = GER_fritz_naphtali_advisor
			custom_effect_tooltip = is_hired
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						has_free_political_advisor_slot = yes
					}
					activate_advisor = GER_fritz_naphtali_advisor
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_naphtali_tt
		}
	}
}

		NOT = {
			has_war_with = FRA
			has_country_flag = GER_schacht_removed
			is_ai = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.113 option gerflavour.113.a"
		name = gerflavour.113.a
		ai_chance = { base = 0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_cuts_debt_tt

		add_stability = -0.06

			idea = GER_austerity_program
			days = 365
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = GER_red_general
				GER_kurt_von_schleicher = { is_second_in_command = yes }
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_schleicher_move_right
			add_to_variable = { GER_schleicher_ideology = -20 }

				mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
				days = -45
			}

			}
			subtract_from_variable = {
				var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty
				value = 20
				tooltip = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty_loss
			}
			clamp_variable = { var = GER_Left_SPD_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
			if = {
				limit = {

					has_country_flag = GER_left_spd_in_coalition
				}
				activate_mission = GER_SPD_Left_rift
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				GER_is_swr_path = yes
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_effect_increases_dkp_tt
			add_to_variable = { GER_swr_coalition_balance = -15 }
			GER_check_swr_coalition_strength = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = gerflavour.113 days = 365 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.113 option gerflavour.113.b"
		name = gerflavour.113.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					GER_is_swr_path = yes
					has_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_government = social_democrat
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = GER_Government_Paralysis }
				}
				effect_tooltip = {
					swap_ideas = {
						remove_idea = GER_paralysis_reduce_5
						add_idea = GER_paralysis_base
					}
				}
				add_to_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor = -0.05 }
				clamp_variable = {
					var = GER_government_paralysis_factor
					max = 0
					min = -1
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_government = social_democrat
					if = {
						limit = { is_ai = no }
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.49 }
					}
					else = {
						check_variable = { GER_government_paralysis_factor < -0.69 }
					}
				}
				country_event = gerspd.53
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_left_chairman
					}
				}
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = GER_Z_loyalty
					value = 10
					tooltip = GER_Z_loyalty_loss
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_Z_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_Z_loyalty < 1 }
						is_in_coalition_with_social_conservative = yes
					}
					activate_mission = GER_SPD_Z_rift
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { is_in_coalition_with_social_liberal = yes }
				subtract_from_variable = {
					var = GER_LVP_loyalty
					value = 15
					tooltip = GER_LVP_loyalty_loss
				}
				clamp_variable = { var = GER_LVP_loyalty min = 0 max = 100 }
				if = {
					limit = {
						check_variable = { GER_LVP_loyalty < 1 }
					}
					activate_mission = GER_SPD_LVP_rift
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_political_power = -75
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
				custom_effect_tooltip = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition_hurts_tt
				add_to_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_r = -3 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht }
			custom_effect_tooltip = {
				localization_key = tooltip_disable_political_advisor
				ADVISOR = GER_hjalmar_schacht
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				retire_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = GER_unlocked_schacht_decision
				}
			}
			activate_targeted_decision = { target = THIS decision = GER_remove_schacht }
			set_country_flag = GER_unlocked_schacht_decision

		}

		name = gerflavour.113.c
		trigger = {
			GER_is_swr_path = yes
			has_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht
		}
		add_political_power = -30
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = tooltip_white_line
			custom_effect_tooltip = GER_zentrum_swr_coalition_hurts_tt
			add_to_variable = { GER_Zentrum_seats_r = -1 }
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = market_liberal
			popularity = 0.01
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = {
			localization_key = tooltip_disable_political_advisor
			ADVISOR = GER_hjalmar_schacht
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			retire_character = GER_hjalmar_schacht
		}
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.115 option gerflavour.115.a"
		name = gerflavour.115.a
		add_war_support = -0.08
		set_country_flag = GER_julius_leber_flag
		subtract_from_variable = {
			var = GER_military_faction_strength
			value = 30
			tooltip = GER_faction_strength_expend
		}
		clamp_variable = { var = GER_military_faction_strength max = 100 min = 0 }
		custom_effect_tooltip = GER_affects_postwar_focus_tt
	}
	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event gerflavour.115 option gerflavour.115.b"
		name = gerflavour.115.b
		add_war_support = 0.05
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_active_mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
			}
			add_days_mission_timeout = {
				mission = GER_SPD_demand_action
				days = -45
			}
		}
	}
}

				}

		}
		text = gerflavour.117.d1
	}
	desc = {

			RUS = {

					has_socialist_government = yes

		}

	}

	id = gerflavour.118

	desc = gerflavour.118.d

	major = yes
	fire_for_sender = no
	is_triggered_only = yes

	trigger = {
		wants_world_news = yes
	}

	show_major = {
		OR = {
			regional_europe_news = yes
			regional_north_america_news = yes
			regional_south_america_news = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gerflavour.118.a
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = no
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gerflavour.118.b
		trigger = {
			has_socialist_government = yes
		}
	}
}

# egg
country_event = { #egg basket
	id = geregg.0

	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		original_tag = GER
		surrender_progress > 0.5
		is_in_faction = yes
		has_war_with = FRA
		has_war_with = RUS
		num_divisions < var:FRA.num_divisions # FRA has more divisions than GER
		num_divisions < var:RUS.num_divisions # RUS has more divisions than GER
		any_owned_state = { # GER still controls at least one coastal state, so the Kaiser can escape.
			is_in_home_area = yes
			is_coastal = yes
			is_controlled_by_ROOT_or_ally = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event geregg.0 option 1"
		if = {
			limit = { GER_is_schleicher_path = yes }
			country_event = { id = geregg.1 days = 5 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { has_government = social_democrat }
			country_event = { id = geregg.3 days = 5 }
		}
		#space for S-W-R eggs goes here
	}
}

country_event = { # egg
	id = geregg.2
	title = geregg.2.t
	desc = geregg.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_march

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event geregg.2 option geregg.2.a"
		name = geregg.2.a
		add_war_support = 0.1
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_populist
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = paternal_autocrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
				long_name = GER_bauer_front_party_long
				name = GER_bauer_front_party
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_populist
				long_name = GER_bauer_front_party_long
				name = GER_bauer_front_party
			}
			GER_waldemar_pabst = { set_nationality = ROOT }
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = paternal_autocrat
			elections_allowed = no
		}
		set_temp_variable = { coalition_partner_var = token:national_populist }
		add_to_coalition = yes
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = GER_max_bauer
			country_leader = {
				desc = GER_max_bauer_leader_desc
				ideology = paternal_autocrat_subtype
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		add_country_leader_role = {
			character = GER_max_bauer
			country_leader = {
				desc = GER_max_bauer_leader_desc
				ideology = national_populist_subtype
			}
			promote_leader = yes
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_waldemar_pabst_sic
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = GER_war
			set_country_flag = GER_bauer_putsch
			GER_wilhelm_iii = { clr_character_flag = show_unit_leader_role } #TODO: revert when bug with country_leader variable is fixed
			GER_rupprecht_von_bayern = { clr_character_flag = show_unit_leader_role } #TODO: revert when bug with country_leader variable is fixed
		}
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		unlock_national_focus = GER_bauer_putsch
	}
}

country_event = { # egg
	id = geregg.4
	title = geregg.4.t
	desc = geregg.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_GER_march

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		log = "[GetLogInfo]: event geregg.4 option geregg.4.a"
		name = geregg.4.a
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = social_democrat
			popularity = 0.1
		}
		GER_hermann_muller = {
			if = {
				limit = { has_ideology = social_democrat_subtype }
				promote_character = social_democrat_subtype
			}
			else = {
				add_country_leader_role = {
					country_leader = {
						desc = GER_hermann_muller_sic_desc
						ideology = social_democrat_subtype
					}
					promote_leader = yes
				}
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GER_hofgeismar_circle = { retire = yes }
			if = {
				limit = { has_idea = GER_SPD_rebellion }
				remove_ideas = GER_SPD_rebellion
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = GER_wilhelm_ii }
				GER_wilhelm_ii = { retire = yes }
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = GER_wilhelm_iii }
				GER_wilhelm_iii = {
					retire = yes
					clr_character_flag = show_unit_leader_role #TODO: revert when bug with country_leader variable is fixed
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_character = GER_rupprecht_von_bayern }
				GER_rupprecht_von_bayern = {
					retire = yes
					clr_character_flag = show_unit_leader_role #TODO: revert when bug with country_leader variable is fixed
				}
			}
			GER_theodor_haubach = { set_nationality = ROOT }
		}
		activate_advisor = GER_theodor_haubach_sic
		set_cosmetic_tag = GER_rep
		set_country_flag = GER_republic_established
		unlock_national_focus = GER_the_republic
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}
